***ensceneren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ensceneren.html>ensceneren</a> (65256)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">inszenieren</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">(mettre) <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> scène</i>. Not borrowed directly from French, as there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">*enscener</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ensceneren.html>ensceneren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stage (in a deceptive manner)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ensceneren.html>ensceneren</a></b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">to <b>stage</b> an accident</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to present, to perform</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ensign.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a> (107084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ensigne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">enseigne</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">īnsignia</i>, nominative plural of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">īnsigne</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">insignia</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ensigns</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A badge of office, rank, or power.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1690</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Waller" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edmund Waller">Edmund <a href = vnd.unilang:waller.html>Waller</a></a>,  <cite>The Maid’s Tragedy, Alter’d by <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waller.html>Waller</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://quod.lib.umich.edu/e/eebo/A67336.0001.001/1:3?rgn=div1;view=fulltext">[1]</a></sup>, page 8:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <b>Ensigns</b> of our Power about <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> bear; / And every <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> pays Tribute to the Fair.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>The lowest grade of commissioned officer in the United States Navy, <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> to a lieutenant <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> grade.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1898</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Winston_Churchill_(novelist)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Winston Churchill (novelist)">Winston Churchill</a>,  chapter 10, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Celebrity" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Celebrity">The Celebrity</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:skipper.html>skipper</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Cooke <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> hired at Far Harbor <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a God-fearing <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> with a <a href = vnd.unilang:luke.html>luke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a> interest in his new billet and employer, and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> only <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> prevailed upon to take charge of the yacht after the offer of an emolument equal to <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a year's sea pay of an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a></b> in the navy.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>A flag or banner carried by military units; a standard or color/colour.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">ancient</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1591</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VI,_Part_1" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VI, Part 1">The First Part of <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Sixt</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act V, scene iv]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Hang up your <b>ensigns</b>, let your <a href = vnd.unilang:drums.html>drums</a> be still,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The principal flag or banner flown by a ship (usually at the stern) to indicate nationality.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1960</b> [a. 120],  Ian Scott-Kilvert,  “Life of Alcibiades”, in  <cite>The Rise and Fall of Athens: Nine Greek <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>Lives</a></cite>, translation of original by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Plutarch" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Plutarch">Plutarch</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">But Alcibiades swiftly <a href = vnd.unilang:ran.html>ran</a> up the Athenian <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a></b> on his flagship and bore down on that part of the Peloponnesian fleet which <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> the advantage and <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> pursuing the Athenians.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Any prominent flag or banner.
<ul><li><b>1667</b>?, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Milton" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Milton">John Milton</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paradise_Lost" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Paradise Lost">Paradise <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>Lost</a></a></i>
<dl><dd>Ten thousand thousand <b>ensigns</b> high advanced.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> commissioned officer in the 18th and 19th centuries whose duty <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> to carry the unit's <a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>See Thesaurus:badge</li></ul>
<p><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:junior.html>junior</a> commissioned officer</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span>
</p>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">coronet</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cavalry equivalent of the infantry <a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">second lieutenant</span> (OF-1), first NATO commissioned officer grade above OF-0 trainee officer</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">ensigns</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ensigning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">ensigned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To designate as by an <a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1610</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ben_Jonson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ben Jonson"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>Ben</a> Jonson</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Speeches_at_Prince_Henry%27s_Barriers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Speeches at Prince Henry | s Barriers">The <a href = vnd.unilang:speeches.html>Speeches</a> at Prince <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a>'s Barriers</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://d.lib.rochester.edu/camelot/text/jonson-speeches-at-prince-henries-barriers">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> but ioyn’d the Roses, that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ensign.html>ensign</a>’d</b> / Particular <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>families</a>, but this hath ioyn’d / The <i><a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>Rose</a></i> and <i>Thistle</i>,</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To distinguish by a mark or ornament.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To distinguish by an ornament, especially by a crown.
<dl><dd><i>Any charge which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a crown immediately above or upon it, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to be <b>ensigned</b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ent.html>ent</a> (57609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:enten.html>ente</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:enten.html>enten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to graft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:enten.html>enten</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">enter</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imputāre</i>.
</p>

***entomoloog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:entomoloog.html>entomoloog</a> (52005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From slightly older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entomologie.html>entomologie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔντομον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éntomon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">insect</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-loog</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entomoloog.html>entomoloog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entomoloog.html>entomologen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entomoloog.html>entomoloogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>entomologist <span class="defdate">[from late 18th c.]</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> entrance</h1><br><a href = vnd.unilang:toegang.html>toegang</a><br><a href = vnd.unilang:ingang.html>ingang</a><br><a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entree</a><br></body> 
***entree.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entree</a> (12781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">entrée</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entree</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entrees</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entreetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>the entry to a house, i.e. the room beyond the front <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a>, from which <a href = vnd.unilang:doors.html>doors</a> to other <a href = vnd.unilang:rooms.html>rooms</a> will typically open.</li>
<li>the right of entrance to a building or <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> where there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no general right of entrance.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (formerly) a savoury served after the fish course and before the main course; (now usually) the starter or the main course itself.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">entry</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">hall</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">vestibule</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">entrance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ingang.html>ingang</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">starter</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorgerecht.html>voorgerecht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">amuse</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:entree.html>entree</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>

***epistel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:epistel.html>epistel</a> (93707)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">epistola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐπιστολή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">epistolḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐπιστέλλω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">epistéllō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I send a message</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐπί</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">epí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">upon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στέλλω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stéllō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I prepare, send</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epistel.html>epistel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epistels.html>epistels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epistel.html>episteltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>epistle; a literary composition in the form of a letter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Christianity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> epistle; one of the <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> included as a book of the New <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a>.</li></ol>

***epsilon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:epsilon.html>epsilon</a> (76142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐψιλόν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">epsilón</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the letter Ε</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epsilon.html>epsilon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epsilon.html>epsilons</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:epsilon.html>epsilonnetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The name for the fifth letter of the Greek alphabet.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The IPA symbol that represents the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/open-mid_front_unrounded_vowel" class="extiw" title="w:open-mid front unrounded vowel">open-mid front unrounded vowel</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An arbitrarily small quantity.</li></ol>

***er.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> (18)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Weak form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></i>, the unstressed form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i> ("there")
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>there <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unspecific to distance</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with a preposition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> him, her, it, them.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ermee.html>ermee</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewerkt.html>gewerkt</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I have worked <b>with it/them</b>.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bergen.html>bergen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boven.html>boven</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>You can see the mountains <b>above it/them</b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> an unstressed variety of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a></i>, used when it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not needed to emphasize the specific location relative to the speaker.</li>
<li>With a preposition, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used instead of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> to create a pronominal adverb. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iro</i>, genitive of the personal pronoun (3rd person plural).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">partitive pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> of them, of those (often not <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> in English)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kinderen.html>kinderen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>My brother <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> three children and I have two. (<i>literally:</i> two of those)</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> see any more (of them).</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***erbarmen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a> (65251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">irbarmēn</i>, with two prefixes <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ir-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">ab-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">armēn</i>. The base verb derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*armāną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*armaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">poor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">arm</i>). The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ontfermen.html>ontfermen</a></i> derives from the same source, with a different prefix.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have mercy, to take pity</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:gerund.html>Gerund</a> of the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:erbarmen.html>erbarmen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>mercy, pity</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">erbarming</span></li></ul>
<hr />
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>ere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">honour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dienst.html>dienst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">service</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êren</i>. <ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to honor/honour, to pay homage/respects.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to (sometimes restore a fiancée's) honor by marriage</li></ol>

***ergens.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> (393)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ergent</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ergen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">irgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iergin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iowergin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*euhwargin</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">hwergin</i> (gt; Middle Low German <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">ergent</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">hwergin</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">iowergin</i> (gt; Middle High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">iergen</i>, gt; German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">irgend</i>), Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hwerġen</i>, Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hvargi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>somewhere, anywhere
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>Ergens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vliegveld.html>vliegveld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tas.html>tas</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My bag <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>somewhere</b> in the airport.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>somehow, in some unspecified way
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>Ergens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vind.html>vind</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leuk.html>leuk</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Somehow</b> I think he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nice.</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>Kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>Is</a> there <b>something</b> I can help you with?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergeren.html>ergeren</a> (16276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">argeren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergeren.html>ergeren</a></i>. </p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ergeren.html>ergeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to annoy, to irritate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be annoyed, to be irritated</li></ol>
